Radar Name Variables File naming convention Format

RCCK, RCMK dBuZ, dBZ, KDP, PhiDP, RhoHV, uKDP, uPhiDP, V, W, ZDR yyyymmddHHMMSS00$Variables.vol Rainbow 5

RCCG, RCHL, RCKT dBZ, V, W yyyymmddHHMMSS00$Variables.vol Rainbow 5
